\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ipv6\+Addr\+To\+String()}{ipv6AddrToString()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \hyperlink{compiler__port_8h_a40bb5262bf908c328fbcfbe5d29d0201}{char\+\_\+t}$\ast$ ipv6\+Addr\+To\+String (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \hyperlink{ipv6_8h_aed0cbc40c61ed5b4fb681ebc55237e89}{Ipv6\+Addr} $\ast$}]{ip\+Addr,  }\item[{\hyperlink{compiler__port_8h_a40bb5262bf908c328fbcfbe5d29d0201}{char\+\_\+t} $\ast$}]{str }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Convert a binary I\+Pv6 address to a string representation. 

Call \hyperlink{ipv6_8c_a96e27d88ffdf1b2ca6fca448dc6b4e7e}{ipv6\+Addr\+To\+String()} to convert an I\+Pv6 address to a text representation. The implementation of \hyperlink{ipv6_8c_a96e27d88ffdf1b2ca6fca448dc6b4e7e}{ipv6\+Addr\+To\+String()} function follows R\+FC 5952 recommendations


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em ip\+Addr} & Binary representation of the I\+Pv6 address \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em str} & N\+U\+L\+L-\/terminated string representing the I\+Pv6 address \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Pointer to the formatted string 
\end{DoxyReturn}

1371    \textcolor{comment}{//If, while processing a received packet, a node encounters a Routing}

1387       \textcolor{comment}{//The node must discard the packet}
1388       \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \hyperlink{error_8h_ac7659d73a8cdedc08e9f566bb406689ca2daa3c161edaa4477d1ae954c2136008}{ERROR\_INVALID\_TYPE};
